### 1. 自然阳光特写肖像提示，适用于 Nano Banana 2

**Author**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne)  **Date**: 2026-03-20  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 结构化提示，用于 Nano Banana 2，旨在生成 Sadie Sink 和 Sydney Sweeney 在自然阳光下的超逼真特写肖像。该提示强调真实感、可见的皮肤纹理、强烈的明暗对比，以及特定的相机设置，以模拟原始智能手机拍摄的效果。

![自然阳光特写肖像提示，适用于 Nano Banana 2](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774074532206_4xxudm_HD2HzQKb0AAI0F9.jpg)
![自然阳光特写肖像提示，适用于 Nano Banana 2](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774074532028_quqnkj_HD2HzO5aMAAaqNV.jpg)

```
{
  "photo_type": "Natural sunlight close-up portrait (raw realistic capture)",

  "subject": {
    "face": {
      "description": "Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact, no reshaping or smoothing"
    },

    "pose_description": "Lying or slightly reclined, head tilted, one hand placed under chin",

    "expression": "neutral soft expression, relaxed lips, natural gaze to side"
  },

  "lighting": {
    "type": "direct natural sunlight",

    "setup": [
      "sunlight entering from window side",
      "partial face illumination",
      "hard light edge with soft falloff"
    ],

    "effects": [
      "bright highlight on cheek and nose",
      "strong natural shadow on opposite side",
      "uneven exposure across face",
      "real sunlight contrast"
    ],

    "color_temperature": "natural daylight 5500K"
  },

  "skin_realism": {
    "details": [
      "visible pores",
      "tiny freckles or marks",
      "natural oil shine",
      "uneven skin tone",
      "no smoothing or blur"
    ]
  },

  "hair": {
    "details": [
      "natural strands visible",
      "slight frizz",
      "not perfectly arranged",
      "light catching individual hairs"
    ]
  },

  "clothing": {
    "details": [
      "white lace top",
      "fine fabric texture visible",
      "small wrinkles and shadows"
    ]
  },

  "accessories": {
    "details": [
      "thin necklace",
      "small pendant",
      "subtle reflections"
    ]
  },

  "camera": {
    "type": "smartphone rear camera",

    "lens": "26mm",

    "settings": {
      "aperture": "f/1.8",
      "iso": "ISO 50-150",
      "shutter_speed": "1/800s"
    },

    "focus": "sharp on eyes, slight falloff",

    "sensor_behavior": [
      "slight grain in shadows",
      "highlight clipping in bright areas",
      "minor noise"
    ]
  },

  "lens_effects": {
    "details": [
      "slight overexposure on highlights",
      "natural contrast",
      "no artificial blur",
      "real depth falloff"
    ]
  },

  "background": {
    "details": [
      "white fabric or bedding",
      "soft folds",
      "light shadows",
      "not perfectly smooth"
    ]
  },

  "color_grading": {
    "style": "raw natural",

    "rules": [
      "no heavy editing",
      "slight warm tint",
      "natural skin tones",
      "real camera color"
    ]
  },

  "imperfections": [
    "lighting unevenness",
    "skin texture",
    "minor grain",
    "highlight burn"
  ],

  "composition": {
    "camera_angle": "close-up slight top angle",
    "framing": "tight face crop",
    "depth": "face sharp, edges softer"
  },

  "resolution_and_aspect_ratio": "4K, 4:5",

  "vibe": "natural beauty, sunlight, effortless realism",

  "strict_rules": {
    "must_have": [
      "real sunlight contrast",
      "skin texture visible",
      "no smoothing",
      "reference face unchanged"
    ],

    "avoid": [
      "studio "
    ]
  }
```

### 2. Nano Banana Pro 室内温馨团体镜面自拍提示词

**Author**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne)  **Date**: 2026-03-20  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 结构化提示，用于让 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张镜面自拍，画面中包含三个人物（包括 Sadie Sink 和 Sydney Sweeney），置于温暖的室内光线中，模仿真实的手机手持拍摄效果。该提示指定了不均匀的光照、可见的皮肤纹理、轻微的颗粒感，并要求提供三张参考图片以确保人物身份的准确性。

![Nano Banana Pro 室内温馨团体镜面自拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774074535928_s9uhmg_HD2FGZZaEAA3ukM.jpg)

```
{
  "photo_type": "Mirror selfie (real iPhone capture, indoor warm lighting)",

  "subjects": {
    "count": 3,

    "faces": {
      "description": "Use 3 uploaded reference images, keep identity exact, no smoothing or reshaping"
    },

    "pose_description": "Center subject holding phone taking mirror selfie, two friends standing slightly behind on each side, not perfectly aligned",

    "expressions": [
      "center: playful expression, slightly open mouth",
      "left: subtle pout, relaxed",
      "right: neutral confident look"
    ],

    "body_language": [
      "natural posture",
      "slight asymmetry",
      "not perfectly posed"
    ]
  },

  "clothing": {
    "details": [
      "center: light beige blazer with matching top and skirt",
      "others: black outfits",
      "real fabric folds and creases visible"
    ]
  },

  "lighting": {
    "type": "bathroom indoor lighting",

    "setup": [
      "overhead warm lights",
      "mirror reflection light bounce",
      "uneven brightness across faces"
    ],

    "effects": [
      "slight overexposure on forehead",
      "shadow under chin",
      "color warmth variation",
      "not evenly lit"
    ],

    "color_temperature": "warm 3200K"
  },

  "phone_capture": {
    "details": [
      "visible phone in hand",
      "slight lens distortion from wide camera",
      "minor perspective stretch",
      "real handheld framing"
    ]
  },

  "camera": {
    "type": "smartphone front/back camera",

    "lens": "26mm wide",

    "settings": {
      "aperture": "f/1.8",
      "iso": "ISO 200-500",
      "shutter_speed": "1/50s"
    },

    "focus": "slightly imperfect focus",

    "sensor_behavior": [
      "minor grain",
      "shadow noise",
      "slight softness"
    ]
  },

  "skin_realism": {
    "details": [
      "visible pores",
      "natural shine",
      "uneven texture",
      "tiny blemishes",
      "no airbrush"
    ]
  },

  "hair": {
    "details": [
      "slight frizz",
      "loose strands",
      "not perfectly styled"
    ]
  },

  "background": {
    "setting": "bathroom mirror",

    "details": [
      "warm wall panels",
      "mirror reflection depth",
      "slight blur and noise",
      "real environment imperfections"
    ]
  },

  "color_grading": {
    "style": "raw phone photo",

    "rules": [
      "no heavy filter",
      "slight yellow tint",
      "natural contrast",
      "not cinematic"
    ]
  },

  "imperfections": [
    "grain",
    "lighting imbalance",
    "minor blur",
    "lens distortion"
  ],

  "composition": {
    "camera_angle": "handheld mirror angle",
    "framing": "slightly off-center",
    "depth": "all subjects visible, slight background softness"
  },

  "resolution_and_aspect_ratio": "4K, 4:5",

  "vibe": "real girls night selfie, casual, unfiltered moment",

  "strict_rules": {
    "must_have": [
      "mirror selfie look"

### 3. Nano Banana Pro 复古闪光灯群拍提示词

**Author**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne)  **Date**: 2026-03-20  **Language**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于让 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张室内派对自拍，其中包含三个人物（Sadie Sink、Sydney Sweeney 和用户），并带有复古闪光灯美学。该提示词指定了刺眼的直射闪光灯照明、紧凑的构图、特定的表情（嘟嘴），以及可见颗粒和皮肤纹理等真实感细节，并要求提供三张参考图像以保留人物身份。

![Nano Banana Pro 复古闪光灯群拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774074533519_qk36kf_HD12P_ubkAAm5yR.jpg)

```
{
  "photo_type": "Indoor party selfie (vintage flash aesthetic, raw realism)",

  "subjects": [
    {
      "id": "person_left",
      "face": {
        "description": "Use reference image 1, keep identity 100% unchanged"
      },
      "pose": "Leaning slightly inward, shoulder angled forward",
      "expression": "Pout lips, slightly squinted eyes, relaxed playful look"
    },
    {
      "id": "person_center",
      "face": {
        "description": "Use reference image 2, keep identity 100% unchanged"
      },
      "pose": "Centered, leaning slightly forward toward camera",
      "expression": "Soft pout lips, relaxed eyes, subtle confidence"
    },
    {
      "id": "person_right",
      "face": {
        "description": "Use reference image 3, keep identity 100% unchanged"
      },
      "pose": "Leaning inward, head slightly tilted toward center",
      "expression": "Pout lips, soft playful expression"
    }
  ],

  "interaction": {
    "body_contact": "tight shoulder-to-shoulder grouping",
    "energy": "casual, playful, close friends"
  },

  "pose_rules": {
    "important": [
      "faces very close together",
      "slight overlap of shoulders",
      "tight crop composition",
      "all subjects angled toward camera"
    ]
  },

  "expression_rules": {
    "important": [
      "all subjects doing pout/kiss face",
      "slight variation in intensity",
      "natural not exaggerated"
    ]
  },

  "lighting": {
    "type": "direct harsh flash",

    "setup": [
      "camera flash from front",
      "dark indoor environment",
      "no soft lighting"
    ],

    "effects": [
      "bright face highlights",
      "flat lighting on skin",
      "strong shadow falloff behind",
      "flash shine on nose and cheeks"
    ],

    "color_temperature": "warm slightly orange tint"
  },

  "camera": {
    "type": "smartphone front camera",

    "lens": "24mm wide",

    "settings": {
      "aperture": "f/2.2",
      "iso": "ISO 700",
      "shutter_speed": "1/60s"
    },

    "lens_behavior": [
      "slight wide distortion",
      "faces closer appear slightly larger",
      "edge softness"
    ],

    "sensor_behavior": [
      "visible grain",
      "color noise",
      "low dynamic range",
      "flash overexposure in highlights"
    ]
  },

  "color_grading": {
    "style": "vintage digital",

    "rules": [
      "warm orange tone",
      "slightly faded blacks",
      "film-like softness",
      "no modern HDR look"
    ]
  },

  "skin_realism": {
    "details": [
      "visible pores",
      "flash shine",
      "minor imperfections",
      "natural texture"
    ]
  },

  "hair": {
    "details": [
      "natural loose styling",
      "slight frizz",
      "individual strands visible",
      "shine from flash"
    ]
  },

  "clothing": {
    "style": "casual night outfits",

    "details": [
      "black tops",
      "denim jeans",
      "s"
    ]
  }

```
{
"prompt": "two world-famous K-pop idols, Rosé and Jennie, in their mid-20s taking a close-up intimate selfie together in a trendy modern beer pub at night, warm ambient golden lighting from overhead lamps and string lights, cozy industrial interior with wooden tables and blurred bokeh background of plants and bar shelves, they are cheek-to-cheek; Rosé on the left has long, straight strawberry blonde hair flowing down past her shoulders, slender features, wearing a sleek black latex miniskirt and a short white cropped top showing her toned midriff, natural glowing makeup with soft rose lips, holding a large tulip glass of golden beer with thick foam head in her right hand, smiling softly with a confident elegant expression; Jennie on the right has long wavy voluminous espresso-brown hair, cat-like eyes, wearing a black latex miniskirt and a fitted black open-knit sheer long-sleeve crop top with small sparkly studs, playful pouty duck-face kissy lips toward camera, both look directly at camera lens, slight head tilt, natural skin texture with subtle highlights, rings on fingers, earrings visible, casual chic Korean street-fashion idol aesthetic, high detail faces, realistic skin pores and hair strands, photorealistic, shot on iPhone 15 Pro in portrait mode with shallow depth of field, soft cinematic color grading, warm tones, cozy atmosphere, ultra-detailed 8k",

![子瑜女仆角色扮演镜面自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773989011828_gm8yd2_HDt6AdfbcAA6ijP.jpg)

{
  "subject": {

  },

  },

    "frame": "Tall and slender, athletic yet feminine frame, defined waist, emphasized by leaning posture",

    "legs": "Long-looking in dark green fishnet stockings"
  },
  "pose": {
    "position": "Standing in front of full-length mirror, arching back slightly while leaning toward the glass",
    "hands": "One holding phone leaving the entire face clearly visible, other gently touching the mirror surface",
    "overall": "Elegant yet playful forward-weighted candid lean"
  },
  "clothing": {
    "top": "Frilly white maid top with emerald green trim, ruffled straps & neckline, small green ribbons",
    "bottom": "Short frilled emerald-green-and-white maid skirt, green fishnet stockings",
    "details": "Matching wrist cuffs, strong emerald-white contrast"
  },
  "accessories": {
    "headwear": "Emerald green ruffled maid headband",
    "jewelry": "Delicate silver necklace with pendant",

### 6. 20 世纪 70 年代复古厨房肖像与 K-Pop 偶像

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于让 Nano Banana 生成一个 1970 年代复古美学厨房场景，其中包含一位 K-Pop 偶像（Sadie Sink、Millie Bobby Brown、Emma Myers 或 Bethany）。它要求使用生物识别参考图像来确定面部结构，指定一个俏皮的姿势（坐在柜台上，眨眼），并详细描述了服装（酒红色和白色连体衣，玛丽珍高跟鞋）和环境（格子防溅板，复古道具，柔光箱摄影灯）。

### 7. 悉尼·斯威尼霓虹加油站场景

**Author**: [Shreya♡](https://x.com/Shreyayadav)  **Date**: 2026-03-19  **Language**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 模型设计的高度结构化 JSON 提示，用于生成一张图片，内容为西德尼·斯威尼（Sydney Sweeney）身穿“Hello Kitty”露脐上衣和迷你裙，在夜晚潮湿的加油站场景中。该提示详细描述了她的特定体型、服装、配饰（包括竖中指手势）、霓虹灯环境，以及广角鱼眼镜头和 9:16 宽高比等技术相机规格。

![悉尼·斯威尼霓虹加油站场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773988989831_4ql42e_HDzEkXYbMAAX8TG.jpg)
![悉尼·斯威尼霓虹加油站场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773988989730_e7z5v9_HDzEkVFa0AA_0al.jpg)
![悉尼·斯威尼霓虹加油站场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773988990271_94utci_HDzEkWmboAIouxh.jpg)

```
{
  "subject": {
    "identity": "Actress {argument name="actress name" default="Sydney Sweeney"},smiling widely.",
    "body": "Hourglass figure with athletic definition. Broad shoulders tapering to a narrow, cinched waist, contrasting with prominent, curvy hips and well-developed glutes (high waist-to-hip ratio). Muscular legs and calves are visible in socks.",
    "wardrobe": {
      "top": "Pink crop top with 'Hello Kitty' text and logo in white and red, and a pink bow.",
      "bottom": "White pleated mini skirt.",

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于生成一张超逼真的中景肖像，描绘的是在室内洗手间场景中的 Sadie Sink，详细说明了她的姿势（双手插在头发中）、服装（红色深 V 连体衣）、灯光（暖色侧光）和情绪（性感、自信）。

![在洗手间为 萨迪·辛克 (Sadie Sink) 绘制肖像的结构化提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927651880_yos6t1_HAAhj-sW4AANf8N.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Sadie sink with long, dark hair pulled back with both hands.",
      "appearance": {
        "skin": "Tan, flawless complexion.",
        "hair": "Dark, voluminous, straight.",
        "makeup": "Full face, bold eye makeup, defined brows, nude lipstick."
      },
      "pose": "Standing, arms raised with hands in her hair, looking slightly away from the camera."
    },
    "attire": {
      "clothing": "Fitted {argument name="bodysuit color" default="red"} plunge neckline bodysuit with a fabric rose detail on the left side.",
      "accessories": "Delicate silver necklace, multiple bracelets on both wrists, small hoop earrings."
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Indoor restroom with grey paneled doors and a large mirror.",
      "details": "Countertop, metal faucet visible in the foreground, reflected light on the mirror."
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "Warm, artificial side lighting.",
      "source": "Visible light source on the right, creating soft shadows and highlighting her form and hair."
    },
    "mood": "Sultry, confident, candid.",
    "camera_details": {
      "style": "Ultra photorealistic.",
      "shot": "Medium shot.",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on the subject.",
      "quality": "High resolution, rich textures, natural colors."
    }
  }
}
```

### 61. 电影级桑拿肖像（神似 Sydney Sweeney）

**Author**: [Yaseen Khan Gul](https://x.com/YaseenK7212)  **Date**: 2026-01-31  **Language**: en

> 一个高度技术化且细节丰富的提示，用于生成一张超现实的电影级肖像，描绘一位酷似西德尼·斯威尼 (Sydney Sweeney) 的女性身处一个超豪华的芬兰桑拿房中。该提示详细说明了人体解剖学上的精确性（可见的皮肤毛孔、水滴）、着装（白色棉质毛巾）、环境（雪松木、热气氤氲），以及复杂的灯光/光学设置（Octane Render、35mm 镜头、f/1.8 光圈）。

![电影级桑拿肖像（神似 Sydney Sweeney）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927671296_a0l7qe_HAAVBWyWAAAO1rk.jpg)
![电影级桑拿肖像（神似 Sydney Sweeney）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927671238_w8qot6_HAAVBXDXAAAeD-d.jpg)
![电影级桑拿肖像（神似 Sydney Sweeney）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927671543_9wfvri_HAAVBW_W8AAu84S.jpg)

```
{
  "project_configuration": {
    "title": "Cinematic Wellness: The Sauna Portrait",
    "version": "2.0_High_Fidelity",
    "output_parameters": {
      "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
      "resolution": "8K UHD",
      "color_space": "DCI-P3",
      "style_preset": "Hyper-realistic Photorealism",
      "rendering_engine": "Octane Render / Unreal Engine 5.4 Path Tracing"
    }
  },
  "subject_composition": {
    "identity": {
      "resemblance": "Sydney Sweeney",
      "age_range": "Early 20s",
      "expression": "Serene, introspective, captivating, direct eye contact",
      "skin_tone": "Fair, ivory, dewy complexion"
    },
    "anatomical_precision": {
      "micro_details": "Visible skin pores, fine vellus hair, realistic skin texture, subcutaneous scattering (SSS), tiny crystalline water droplets on collarbones and forehead.",
      "eyes": "Deep hazel, intricate iris patterns, sharp catchlights reflecting the warm sauna interior.",
      "lips": "Soft pink, moist, slightly parted, high-gloss finish from the humidity.",
      "hair": "Long blonde hair, wet-look styling, damp strands clinging to the skin, dark-blonde roots, high-specularity sheen."
    },
    "attire_and_fabric": {
      "primary_garment": "High-texture white cotton bath towel",
      "fabric_details": "Visible terry cloth loops, heavy fabric weight, damp patches showing darker white tones, intricate weaving patterns, soft frayed edges."
    },
    "pose_and_dynamics": {
      "position": "Seated elegantly on a mid-level cedar bench, legs crossed at the ankles.",
      "body_language": "Leaning slightly forward to create depth, relaxed shoulders, natural posture, hands resting softly on the wood."
    },
    "environment_design": {
      "setting": "Ultra-luxury traditional Finnish sauna",
      "interior_materials": {
        "wood": "Polished Western Red Cedar, horizontal slats, visible grain, knots, and heat-induced oil sheen.",
        "elements": "Hot sauna stones in a stainless steel heater (background), rising heat haze."
      },
      "atmospheric_effects": {
        "steam": "Ethereal swirling mist, volumetric fog, thick humidity, moisture-laden air.",
        "haze": "Soft-focus background, golden-hour glow filtered through steam particles."
      }
    },
    "lighting_and_optics": {
      "lighting_setup": {
        "type": "Warm diffused ambient lighting",
        "primary_source": "Hidden LED strips beneath benches creating a soft under-glow.",
        "secondary_source": "Top-down warm spotlighting (3200K temperature).",
        "shadows": "Soft, diffused, zero harsh edges."
      },
      "optical_settings": {
        "lens": "35mm prime lens, wide angle with minimal distortion.",
        "aperture": "f/1.8 for shallow depth of field (bokeh background).",
        "focus": "Sharp focus on the subject's eyes, gradual fall-off on the shoulders and environment."
      }
    }
  }
}
```

    {
      "entity_type": "person",

      "biometrics": {
        "skin": {
          "tone": "fair",

        },
        "hair": {
          "color": "light brown",

          }
        ]
      },

            }

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成安雅·泰勒-乔伊 (Anya Taylor-Joy) 的阳光亲吻、空灵肖像，重点突出黄金时段的阳光。该提示指定了她金色的金发、明显的雀斑、淡紫色花卉紧身胸衣上衣，以及头部靠在手上的姿势。光线至关重要，在黑暗、失焦的背景下营造出高对比度和暖色调。

```
{
  "prompt_data": {
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "woman Anya Taylor-Joy 
      "hair": {
        "color": "Golden blonde with lighter platinum highlights",
        "style": "Long, straight to slightly wavy, loose and messy, falling over shoulders",

      },

        "lips": "Natural pink shade, slightly parted, soft pout",
        "expression": "Smiling, direct eye contact with the lens"
      }
    },
    "clothing": {
      "item": "Floral corset-style top or bustier",
      "color": "Lavender",
      "pattern": "Small vintage yellow rose print with green leaves",
      "details": "Spaghetti straps, lace trim detailing"
    },
    "pose": {
      "action": "Head resting heavily on right hand",

      "angle": "Close-up portrait, selfie angle, slight tilt of the head"
    },
    "lighting_and_atmosphere": {
      "type": "Golden hour sunlight, natural direct lighting",
      "direction": "Side lighting coming from the left (viewer's perspective), casting distinct shadows on the right side of the face and background",
      "mood": "Sun-kissed, ethereal, warm, intimate, summer afternoon vibe",
      "shadows": "High contrast between the bright sunlit skin and the dark background shadows"
    },
    "background": {
      "setting": "Luxury Indoor domestic setting",
      "details": "Dark, out-of-focus background, hints of a pink door with vertical panels",
      "depth_of_field": "Shallow depth of field, blurring the background to isolate the subject"
    },

      "quality": "4k HD, ultra-realistic, highly detailed",

Before-and-after upper-body portrait photo of Sydney Sweeney, smiling in both images, split vertically down the center into two equal halves for a direct visual comparison. Clear text labels appear at the top of each half.

Left side – “Day” (label at top):
Natural, no makeup look. Realistic skin texture with visible pores, slight under-eye shadows, natural lips, minimal grooming. Soft, relaxed smile. Hair casually styled. She is wearing a simple nightgown for bed, comfortable and modest. Daytime feeling, fresh and unstyled, authentic at-home appearance.

Professional makeup applied: even skin tone, subtle contouring, enhanced eyes with mascara and eyeliner, defined brows, soft lipstick. Bright, confident smile. Hair styled elegantly. She is wearing a beautiful, pink dress with a deep neckline

Photography & Camera Style:
Smartphone camera realism, portrait mode look, handheld feel, natural lighting, slight digital noise, mild compression artifacts, realistic color balance, minimal retouching, honest skin detail. Casual but clear comparison photo rather than studio perfection.

Aspect ratio:
3:4 (portrait)

### 126. 足球视频游戏胜利场景，C 罗和梅西提示

**Author**: [A.D.BARRY](https://x.com/aiwithadb)  **Date**: 2026-01-06  **Language**: en

> 一个复杂、叙事驱动的提示，用于拍摄一张超现实的电影级照片，捕捉现代公寓中一个幽默、非摆拍的瞬间。场景中，主要人物（身份已从参考照片中锁定）正在庆祝一场压倒性的视频游戏胜利（镜面反射中可见 10-5 的比分），而克里斯蒂亚诺·罗纳尔多则表现出竞争性的愤怒，莱昂内尔·梅西和基利安·姆巴佩则随意地观察并吃着零食。

![足球视频游戏胜利场景，C 罗和梅西提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804018340_x8oo7c_G-AMY5iXkAA_Cio.jpg)

```
A hyper-realistic, ultra-detailed 8K cinematic photograph captured with a 35mm lens, medium-wide shot, set inside a realistic, modern apartment living room with a natural, lived-in home atmosphere.
Scene logic & composition:
The TV is positioned directly in front of the players and remains outside the camera frame.
A large decorative mirror on the wall subtly reflects the TV screen, clearly showing the final match result.
In the mirror reflection, the football video game result screen displays a crushing score: {argument name="winning score" default="10"} – {argument name="losing score" default="5"}, clearly in favor of the main subject.
The numbers are bold, bright, and unmistakable against a green pitch and stadium crowd background.
In the foreground, the main subject (uploaded 100% face as reference, identity fully locked and preserved) is seated on a comfortable couch, body oriented straight toward the unseen TV. He is wearing a relaxed home tracksuit , calm and confident, with a controlled victorious expression after the dominant win holding a PlayStation controller while smiling .
Seated next to him on the couch is {argument name="losing player" default="Cristiano Ronaldo"}, holding a PlayStation controller tightly.
His body language shows clear frustration and anger: tense jaw, furrowed brows, clenched fists, shoulders tight, leaning forward aggressively.
His expression communicates competitive rage and disbelief after losing so badly.
Standing slightly behind and to the side of the couch is Lionel Messi and Mbappe, relaxed and casual, eating food from a plate while watching the scene.
He is smiling subtly, enjoying the moment, completely calm and unbothered, creating a strong contrast with Ronaldo’s anger and adding humor and human warmth to the scene.
A realistic coffee table sits between the couch and the TV, filled with casual home snacks and drinks: pizza slices, chips, sandwiches, and soft drinks, slightly messy to enhance realism.
Lighting is soft, cinematic, and natural, combining ambient room light with the reflected TV glow from the mirror, which subtly illuminates faces and hands.
Depth of field keeps the faces and mirror reflection sharp while softly blurring background elements.

### 199. 闪光灯人像摄影：砖墙背景

**Author**: [Lex](https://x.com/lexx_aura)  **Date**: 2026-02-07  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 生成一张高对比度、坦率的年轻女性肖像（类似于 Sydney Sweeney 或 Billie Eilish），她身穿俏皮的服装（豹纹短裤、打结 T 恤），斜靠在老旧的砖墙上，利用直射闪光摄影营造戏剧性的阴影。

![闪光灯人像摄影：砖墙背景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770532815443_l8i4hw_HAiSux8XkAAVpwC.jpg)
![闪光灯人像摄影：砖墙背景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770532815475_oaxnw8_HAiSux_WwAAeXxP.jpg)
![闪光灯人像摄影：砖墙背景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770532815602_ub43n1_HAiSux_W8AALFFp.jpg)

```
{
  "image_description": {
    "subject": {
      "type": "Young woman",
      "pose": "Standing, leaning back against a textured brick wall. Both arms are raised with hands touching the back of her head/hair. Torso is slightly arched, head tilted slightly.",
      "hair": "Long, reddish-brown (auburn) hair with bangs, falling past shoulders.",
      "facial_features": {
        "expression": "Smiling broadly with open mouth, teeth visible, looking slightly off-camera.",
        "details": "Fair skin with visible freckles, dark eyeliner, defined eyebrows, reddish lip color."
      },
      "attire": {
        "top": "White short-sleeved t-shirt, tied in a knot at the front waist to expose the midriff.",
        "bottom": "Leopard print mini shorts with a sequined or textured finish.",
        "accessories": [
          "Thick black belt with silver grommets/studs worn low on the hips",
          "Silver chain bracelets on both wrists",
          "Thin necklace with a star pendant",
          "Red thigh-high leg warmer or sock visible on the left leg"
        ]
      }
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Indoor location with rustic aesthetic (possibly a bar, hallway, or restaurant).",
      "background_elements": {
        "wall": "Exposed aged brick wall with varying reddish-brown tones.",
        "art": "Framed painting hanging on the left wall, resembling Gustav Klimt's 'The Kiss' (gold and patterned tones)."
      },
      "lighting": "Warm ambient lighting mixed with direct flash photography, creating a high-contrast shadow behind the subject on the brick wall."
    },
    "technical_quality": {
      "resolution": "4K Ultra HD",
      "style": "Flash photography, candid portrait, vibrant colors, sharp focus on subject, slight vignette effect.",
      "texture": "High detail on fabric textures (sequins, cotton) and brick surface."
    }
  }
}
```

### 200. Sadie Sink 风格：淡粉色连衣裙搭配运动鞋的镜面自拍

**Author**: [Rowan](https://x.com/rowanali09)  **Date**: 2026-02-07  **Language**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张全身镜面自拍照，灵感来自 Sadie Sink 的形象。该提示指定了俏皮的表情、柔和的粉色褶皱迷你连衣裙、高帮篮球运动鞋（深摩卡配色）和一条粗大的串珠项链，场景设置在室内走廊，光线柔和自然。

![Sadie Sink 风格：淡粉色连衣裙搭配运动鞋的镜面自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770532792177_f8aqm3_HAiHVzgaIAAbvcH.jpg)

        "fit": "Bodycon, tight-fitting",
